[呼吁书《彻查徐州铁链女事件 保障公民免于恐惧的自由》及联署名单 1932人](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/1932.html)
------

<div>
<span><a name='more'></a></span><p><br /></p><p><b>签名推特：<span lang="EN-GB">@shudong1984</span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US">签名电报：</span><span lang="EN-GB">@shudong1984<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US">更新时间</span><span lang="EN-GB"> 2022</span><span lang="EN-US">年</span><span lang="EN-GB">4</span><span lang="EN-US">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">20</span><span lang="EN-US">日</span><span lang="EN-GB"> 4:32</span>&nbsp;</b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">徐州铁链女事件的真相和处置事关每一位中国公民的权利保障，事关社会整体的正义与进步，我们强烈呼吁：</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">1.</span><span style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">由中央政府部门组成联合调查组，作出公正、公开、具有社会信服力的真相调查。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">2.</span><span style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">依法追究徐州铁链女事件中渎职的各级公职人员，依法惩治贩卖、残害妇女的刑事犯罪人员。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">3.</span><span style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">全国范围内开展人口贩卖犯罪活动的普查、打击，对被拐卖、受害的妇女儿童进行解救和社会救助。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span>联署名单（实名，居住地）<span lang="EN-GB">1932</span>人：</b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">1 </span><span lang="EN-GB">23</span>日邮件被拒收退回。</b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">二、<span lang="EN-GB">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-GB">3</span>月<span lang="EN-GB">8</span>日中午，整理者一式两份打印了<span lang="EN-GB">1878</span>位签名者的联署名单，通过<span lang="EN-GB">EMS</span>邮寄，分别于<span lang="EN-GB">3</span>月<span lang="EN-GB">9</span>日<span lang="EN-GB">08:53</span>被国家信访局、<span lang="EN-GB">3</span>月<span lang="EN-GB">10</span>日<span lang="EN-GB">07</span>：<span lang="EN-GB">52</span>被全国人大常委会办公厅签收。</span>&nbsp;</b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"><b>三、联署的整理及投递人至今没有收到以上两份邮件的回信。</b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"></p><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a
